defined by ShutdownDelayDuration to detect that /readyz is red\n\t\t// and stop sending traffic to this server.\n\t\tshutdownInitiatedCh.Signal()\n\t\tklog.V(1).InfoS(\"[graceful-termination] shutdown long running requests) have been drained.\n\t\t// - once drained, http Server Shutdown is invoked with a timeout of 2s,\n\t\t//   net/http waits for 1s for the peer to respond to a GO_AWAY frame, the WithWaitGroup filter. Key cleanup ordering observed:\\n1. Termination handler signals goroutines via context cancellation\\n2. Scrape discovery manager stops (cancelScrape())\\n3. Notify discovery manager stops (cancelNotify())\\n4. Rule manager stops before scrape manager to prevent incomplete rule evaluations\\n5. ShutdownDelayDuration (configurable) allows load balancers to detect /readyz failure and drain connections\\n3. PreShutdownHooks execute to deregister from service discovery\\n4. After draining completes, http.Server.Shutdown() is invoked with ShutdownTimeout (2 seconds when ShutdownSendRetryAfter is enabled)\\n6. Key cleanup ordering observed:\\n1. Termination handler signals goroutines via context cancellation\\n2. Scrape discovery manager stops (cancelScrape())\\n3. Notify discovery manager stops (cancelNotify())\\n4. Rule manager stops before scrape manager to prevent incomplete rule evaluations\\n5. Logs timeout errors if graceful shutdown exceeds 30 seconds\\n4.
